# Context Orchestrator v2

Orquestrador de contexto baseado em retrieval seletivo por tags, decay scoring,
attention sinks, e retrieval progressivo (SwiftMem + MemGPT + A-MEM + MemoryBank +
StreamingLLM + Stanford Generative Agents + ByteRover + ITR + WISE).

---

## Protocolo de Boot (executar na primeira mensagem)

### Passo 1 — Classificar a tarefa

Ler a primeira mensagem do usuario e classificar em um ou mais perfis:

| Perfil | Palavras-chave de match | Tags MEMORY.md |
|--------|------------------------|----------------|
| `juridico` | processo, caso, cliente, CNJ, OAB, peticao, audiencia, prazo | `#juridico` |
| `vault` | vault, obsidian, nota, pasta, template, frontmatter, diario, governanca | `#vault #governanca` |
| `bot` | capivara, whatsapp, webhook, evolution, piper, tts, telefone | `#bot` |
| `infra` | vps, docker, container, deploy, gcp, nginx, traefik, ssh, servidor | `#infraestrutura` |
| `rag` | embedding, semantica, neo4j, colbert, ner, busca, indexacao | `#rag` |
| `codigo` | bug, feature, refactor, teste, api, endpoint, funcao, modulo | (nenhuma memoria especifica) |
| `geral` | (nenhum match acima) | somente Core |

### Passo 2 — Retrieval com Decay Scoring (Tsinghua MemoryBank + Stanford)

Abrir `MEMORY.md` (ja esta no contexto). Filtrar por tags do perfil detectado.
Ranquear usando formula composta:

```
score = (0.4 * tag_relevance) + (0.3 * imp/5) + (0.3 * recency_score)

Onde:
  tag_relevance = 1.0 se tag faz match direto, 0.5 se tag pai faz match
  imp = campo imp: do MEMORY.md (1-5), normalizado para 0-1
  recency_score = max(0, 1 - dias_desde_modified/90)
    → arquivo acessado hoje = 1.0
    → arquivo de 30 dias atras = 0.67
    → arquivo de 90+ dias = 0.0 (candidato a archival/prune)
```

```
REGRA: Carregar NO MAXIMO 3-5 arquivos por sessao (score > 0.4).
REGRA: Itens [CORE] so carregam se NENHUM perfil especifico fizer match.
REGRA: Itens #desativado NUNCA carregam automaticamente.
REGRA: Ao carregar um arquivo, atualizar seu frontmatter:
       modified: (data de hoje)
       Isso renova a recency e evita decay excessivo.
```

Exemplo de filtragem (SQL-like com scoring):
```sql
SELECT file, (0.4*tag_match + 0.3*imp/5 + 0.3*recency) AS score
FROM MEMORY
WHERE tags INTERSECT (#bot)
  AND tier != 'archival'
ORDER BY score DESC
LIMIT 3;
```

### Passo 3 — Carregar tools por ITR per-step (95% token reduction)

NAO fazer ToolSearch de todos os tools. Aplicar **Instruction-Tool Retrieval (ITR)**:
a cada PASSO da tarefa, carregar SOMENTE os tools necessarios para aquele passo.

```
REGRA CRITICA: Nunca fazer ToolSearch("computer-use") a menos que
o usuario EXPLICITAMENTE peca para controlar a tela.
28+ tools de computer-use = ~3000 tokens desperdicados.

REGRA: Nunca fazer ToolSearch em lote ("*" ou queries amplas).
REGRA: Um servidor MCP por vez, sob demanda, quando o passo exigir.
REGRA: Antes de fazer ToolSearch, perguntar: "Este passo PRECISA
       deste tool, ou posso resolver com Read/Write/Edit/Bash/Grep/Glob?"
```

| Perfil | Tools permitidos via ToolSearch | Bloqueados por padrao |
|--------|-------------------------------|----------------------|
| `juridico` | Docling, Calendar, Gmail | computer-use, Chrome, Preview, Drive |
| `vault` | nenhum extra | TODOS os MCPs |
| `bot` | nenhum extra | TODOS os MCPs |
| `infra` | nenhum extra | TODOS os MCPs |
| `rag` | nenhum extra | computer-use, Chrome, Calendar |
| `codigo` | nenhum extra | computer-use, Chrome, Docling |
| `geral` | sob demanda | TODOS por padrao |

**Tool Usage Log** (Berkeley BFCL V4): manter mentalmente uma lista de tools
ja carregados nesta sessao. Nunca fazer ToolSearch de um tool ja carregado.

### Passo 4 — Orcamento de contexto com Attention Sinks (MIT StreamingLLM)

**Principio dos Attention Sinks (MIT Han Lab):** LLMs ancoram atencao
desproporcional nos tokens iniciais do contexto. Ao compactar:

```
REGRA ATTENTION SINK: Nunca descartar o system prompt, CLAUDE.md,
e o MEMORY.md durante compactacao. Eles sao os "attention sinks" —
ancoras que orientam todo o comportamento subsequente.

REGRA: Ao compactar conversa, preservar:
  1. System prompt + CLAUDE.md (cabeca — attention sink)
  2. Ultimos 5-8 turnos (cauda — contexto imediato)
  3. Descartar turnos intermediarios primeiro (meio)
  Isso segue o padrao head+tail do StreamingLLM.
```

Budget estimado:

| Componente | Tokens | Tier (WISE) | Compactavel? |
|------------|--------|-------------|-------------|
| System prompt | ~5000 | Imutavel | Nao |
| CLAUDE.md + MEMORY.md | ~3000 | Imutavel | Nao |
| Deferred tool names | ~2000 | Imutavel | Nao |
| Skills list | ~2000 | Imutavel | Parcial |
| Tool schemas carregados | ~500-3000 | Mutavel | Sim (evitar carregar) |
| Memorias carregadas | ~1000-5000 | Mutavel | Sim (max 3-5 arquivos) |
| Conversa | cresce | Mutavel | Sim (compactacao auto) |
| **Budget total** | ~200000 | — | — |

---

## Tiers de Memoria (Zhejiang WISE + USTC MemoryLLM)

Cada arquivo de memoria pertence a um tier:

| Tier | Descricao | Carregamento | Exemplos |
|------|-----------|-------------|----------|
| **Imutavel** | Regras e identidade que nunca mudam | Sempre (via CLAUDE.md) | Estilo, perfil, vault precedencia |
| **Core** | Estado ativo dos projetos principais | Sob demanda por tag match | project_whatsapp_bot, project_vault |
| **Recall** | Projetos secundarios e feedback especifico | Sob demanda se score > 0.4 | feedback_mermaid, project_gcp |
| **Archival** | Projetos desativados, historico | Nunca automatico | project_qwen4b, project_pdf_annotator |

```
REGRA: Tiers sao determinados pelo campo imp: no MEMORY.md:
  imp:5 = Imutavel ou Core (sempre/quase-sempre relevante)
  imp:4 = Core (carrega quando perfil faz match)
  imp:3 = Recall (carrega se score > 0.4)
  imp:2 = Recall (carrega sob demanda explicita)
  imp:1 = Archival (nunca carrega automaticamente)
```

---

## Retrieval Progressivo em 3 Niveis (ByteRover Context Tree)

Resolver queries no nivel mais raso possivel antes de carregar mais contexto:

```
Nivel 1 — MEMORY.md index (ja no contexto, ~70 linhas)
  → Responde: "que projetos existem?", "qual tag usar?", "onde fica X?"
  → Se resolve aqui, NAO carregar nenhum arquivo.

Nivel 2 — Carregar 1-3 arquivos por tag match (score > 0.5)
  → Responde: "qual o estado do bot?", "como funciona o vault?"
  → Ler SOMENTE os arquivos top-ranked.

Nivel 3 — Carregar arquivos auxiliares + ponteiros para vault
  → Responde: "preciso dos detalhes da arquitetura X"
  → Ler ponteiros em project_vault_state.md para arquivos do vault
  → Ou usar Agent tool para pesquisa profunda (nao infla contexto principal)
```

```
REGRA: Maioria das queries resolve no Nivel 1 ou 2.
REGRA: Nivel 3 so com necessidade confirmada.
REGRA: Se Nivel 3 envolver leitura de >3 arquivos, usar Agent tool
       (subagente tem contexto proprio, protege o principal).
```

# /graphify

Turn any folder of files into a navigable knowledge graph with community detection, an honest audit trail, and three outputs: interactive HTML, GraphRAG-ready JSON, and a plain-language GRAPH_REPORT.md.

## Usage

```
/graphify                                             # full pipeline on current directory → Obsidian vault
/graphify <path>                                      # full pipeline on specific path
/graphify https://github.com/<owner>/<repo>           # clone repo then run full pipeline on it
/graphify https://github.com/<owner>/<repo> --branch <branch>  # clone a specific branch
/graphify <url1> <url2> ...                           # clone multiple repos, build each, merge into one cross-repo graph
/graphify <path> --mode deep                          # thorough extraction, richer INFERRED edges
/graphify <path> --update                             # incremental - re-extract only new/changed files
/graphify <path> --directed                            # build directed graph (preserves edge direction: source→target)
/graphify <path> --whisper-model medium                # use a larger Whisper model for better transcription accuracy
/graphify <path> --cluster-only                       # rerun clustering on existing graph
/graphify <path> --no-viz                             # skip visualization, just report + JSON
/graphify <path> --html                               # (HTML is generated by default - this flag is a no-op)
/graphify <path> --svg                                # also export graph.svg (embeds in Notion, GitHub)
/graphify <path> --graphml                            # export graph.graphml (Gephi, yEd)
/graphify <path> --neo4j                              # generate graphify-out/cypher.txt for Neo4j
/graphify <path> --neo4j-push bolt://localhost:7687   # push directly to Neo4j
/graphify <path> --mcp                                # start MCP stdio server for agent access
/graphify <path> --watch                              # watch folder, auto-rebuild on code changes (no LLM needed)
/graphify <path> --wiki                               # build agent-crawlable wiki (index.md + one article per community)
/graphify <path> --obsidian --obsidian-dir ~/vaults/my-project  # write vault to custom path (e.g. existing vault)
/graphify add <url>                                   # fetch URL, save to ./raw, update graph
/graphify add <url> --author "Name"                   # tag who wrote it
/graphify add <url> --contributor "Name"              # tag who added it to the corpus
/graphify query "<question>"                          # BFS traversal - broad context
/graphify query "<question>" --dfs                    # DFS - trace a specific path
/graphify query "<question>" --budget 1500            # cap answer at N tokens
/graphify path "AuthModule" "Database"                # shortest path between two concepts
/graphify explain "SwinTransformer"                   # plain-language explanation of a node
```

## What graphify is for

Drop any folder of code, docs, papers, images, or video into graphify and get a queryable knowledge graph. Persistent across sessions, honest audit trail (EXTRACTED/INFERRED/AMBIGUOUS), community detection surfaces cross-document connections you wouldn't think to ask about.

## What You Must Do When Invoked

If no path was given, use `.` (current directory). Do not ask the user for a path.

If the path argument starts with `https://github.com/` or `http://github.com/`, treat it as a GitHub URL — run Step 0 before anything else, then continue with the resolved local path.

Follow these steps in order. Do not skip steps.

### Step 0 - Clone GitHub repo(s) (only if a GitHub URL was given)

**Single repo:**
```bash
LOCAL_PATH=$(graphify clone <github-url> [--branch <branch>])
# Use LOCAL_PATH as the target for all subsequent steps
```

**Multiple repos (cross-repo graph):**
```bash
# Clone each repo, run the full pipeline on each, then merge
graphify clone <url1>   # → ~/.graphify/repos/<owner1>/<repo1>
graphify clone <url2>   # → ~/.graphify/repos/<owner2>/<repo2>
# Run /graphify on each local path to produce their graph.json files
# Then merge:
graphify merge-graphs \
  ~/.graphify/repos/<owner1>/<repo1>/graphify-out/graph.json \
  ~/.graphify/repos/<owner2>/<repo2>/graphify-out/graph.json \
  --out graphify-out/cross-repo-graph.json
```

Graphify clones into `~/.graphify/repos/<owner>/<repo>` and reuses existing clones on repeat runs. Each node in the merged graph carries a `repo` attribute so you can filter by origin.

### Step 1 - Ensure graphify is installed

```bash
# Detect the correct Python interpreter (handles uv tool, pipx, venv, system installs)
PYTHON=""
GRAPHIFY_BIN=$(which graphify 2>/dev/null)
# 1. uv tool installs — most reliable on modern Mac/Linux
if [ -z "$PYTHON" ] && command -v uv >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    _UV_PY=$(uv tool run graphifyy python -c "import sys; print(sys.executable)" 2>/dev/null)
    if [ -n "$_UV_PY" ]; then PYTHON="$_UV_PY"; fi
fi
# 2. Read shebang from graphify binary (pipx and direct pip installs)
if [ -z "$PYTHON" ] && [ -n "$GRAPHIFY_BIN" ]; then
    _SHEBANG=$(head -1 "$GRAPHIFY_BIN" | tr -d '#!')
    case "$_SHEBANG" in
        *[!a-zA-Z0-9/_.-]*) ;;
        *) "$_SHEBANG" -c "import graphify" 2>/dev/null && PYTHON="$_SHEBANG" ;;
    esac
fi
# 3. Fall back to python3
if [ -z "$PYTHON" ]; then PYTHON="python3"; fi
"$PYTHON" -c "import graphify" 2>/dev/null || "$PYTHON" -m pip install graphifyy -q 2>/dev/null || "$PYTHON" -m pip install graphifyy -q --break-system-packages 2>&1 | tail -3
# Write interpreter path for all subsequent steps (persists across invocations)
mkdir -p graphify-out
"$PYTHON" -c "import sys; open('graphify-out/.graphify_python', 'w').write(sys.executable)"
# Save scan root so `graphify update` (no args) knows where to look next time
echo "$(cd INPUT_PATH && pwd)" > graphify-out/.graphify_root
```

If the import succeeds, print nothing and move straight to Step 2.

**In every subsequent bash block, replace `python3` with `$(cat graphify-out/.graphify_python)` to use the correct interpreter.**

### Step 2 - Detect files

```bash
$(cat graphify-out/.graphify_python) -c "
import json
from graphify.detect import detect
from pathlib import Path
result = detect(Path('INPUT_PATH'))
print(json.dumps(result))
" > graphify-out/.graphify_detect.json
```

Replace INPUT_PATH with the actual path the user provided. Do NOT cat or print the JSON - read it silently and present a clean summary instead:

```
Corpus: X files · ~Y words
  code:     N files (.py .ts .go ...)
  docs:     N files (.md .txt ...)
  papers:   N files (.pdf ...)
  images:   N files
  video:    N files (.mp4 .mp3 ...)
```

Omit any category with 0 files from the summary.

Then act on it:
- If `total_files` is 0: stop with "No supported files found in [path]."
- If `skipped_sensitive` is non-empty: mention file count skipped, not the file names.
- If `total_words` > 2,000,000 OR `total_files` > 200: show the warning and the top 5 subdirectories by file count, then ask which subfolder to run on. Wait for the user's answer before proceeding.
- Otherwise: proceed directly to Step 2.5 if video files were detected, or Step 3 if not.

### Step 2.5 - Transcribe video / audio files (only if video files detected)

Skip this step entirely if `detect` returned zero `video` files.

Video and audio files cannot be read directly. Transcribe them to text first, then treat the transcripts as doc files in Step 3.

**Strategy:** Read the god nodes from `graphify-out/.graphify_detect.json` (or the analysis file if it exists from a previous run). You are already a language model — write a one-sentence domain hint yourself from those labels. Then pass it to Whisper as the initial prompt. No separate API call needed.

**However**, if the corpus has *only* video files and no other docs/code, use the generic fallback prompt: `"Use proper punctuation and paragraph breaks."`

**Step 1 - Write the Whisper prompt yourself.**

Read the top god node labels from detect output or analysis, then compose a short domain hint sentence, for example:

- Labels: `transformer, attention, encoder, decoder` → `"Machine learning research on transformer architectures and attention mechanisms. Use proper punctuation and paragraph breaks."`
- Labels: `kubernetes, deployment, pod, helm` → `"DevOps discussion about Kubernetes deployments and Helm charts. Use proper punctuation and paragraph breaks."`

Set it as `WHISPER_PROMPT` to use in the next command.

    68	    // v2.0 — Apple Cloud Private (PCC) routing. v1.15: o routing real é decidido
    69	    // pela Apple (sem API pública de controle/inspeção). Estes modos só controlam
    70	    // a PERMISSÃO enviada no header; o daemon sinaliza POSSIBILIDADE de cloud.
    71	    // pccMode: 'off' | 'opt-in' | 'auto'
    72	    //   'off'    → no PCC permission header sent; on-device only
    73	    //   'opt-in' → header X-Zeus-Allow-Pcc:1; Apple decides per request
    74	    //   'auto'   → header X-Zeus-Allow-Pcc:auto; daemon flags possibility when load exceeds on-device
    75	    // v1.15 — codex #5: "used" virou "possible". O daemon NÃO consegue medir uso
    76	    // real de PCC (Apple não expõe API de inspeção); só estima possibilidade. Os
    77	    // campos refletem honestamente "cloud era possível", não "cloud foi usado".
    78	    this.pccMode = 'off';
    79	    this.lastPccPossible = false;      // updated from response header X-Zeus-Pcc-Possible
    80	    this.pccPossibleCount = 0;         // total requests onde cloud era possível (heurística)
    81	  }
    82	
    83	  setPccMode(mode) {
    84	    const valid = ['off', 'opt-in', 'auto'];
    85	    this.pccMode = valid.includes(mode) ? mode : 'off';
    86	  }
    87	
    88	  getPccStatus() {
    89	    return {
    90	      mode: this.pccMode,
    91	      lastPossible: this.lastPccPossible,
    92	      possibleCount: this.pccPossibleCount,
    93	    };
    94	  }
    95	
    96	  /**
    97	   * Snapshot of current metrics + estimated token cost.
    98	   * Heuristic: 1 token ~= 4 bytes for English/Portuguese text (very rough).
    99	   */
   100	  getMetrics() {
   101	    const byEndpoint = {};
   102	    for (const [k, v] of this.metrics.byEndpoint) {
   103	      byEndpoint[k] = {
   104	        count: v.count,
   105	        bytesIn: v.bytesIn,
   106	        bytesOut: v.bytesOut,
   107	        estimatedTokens: Math.round((v.bytesIn + v.bytesOut) / 4),
   108	      };
   109	    }
   110	    return {
   111	      requests: this.metrics.requests,
   112	      bytesIn: this.metrics.bytesIn,
   113	      bytesOut: this.metrics.bytesOut,
   114	      estimatedTokens: Math.round((this.metrics.bytesIn + this.metrics.bytesOut) / 4),
   115	      byEndpoint,
   116	      sinceMs: Date.now() - this.metrics.startedAt,
   117	    };
   118	  }
   119	
   120	  resetMetrics() {
   121	    this.metrics = {
   122	      requests: 0,
   123	      bytesIn: 0,
   124	      bytesOut: 0,
   125	      byEndpoint: new Map(),
   126	      startedAt: Date.now(),
   127	    };
   128	  }
   129	
   130	  _recordMetric(endpoint, bytesOut, bytesIn) {
   131	    this.metrics.requests++;
   132	    this.metrics.bytesOut += bytesOut;
   133	    this.metrics.bytesIn += bytesIn;
   134	    let row = this.metrics.byEndpoint.get(endpoint);
   135	    if (!row) { row = { count: 0, bytesIn: 0, bytesOut: 0 }; this.metrics.byEndpoint.set(endpoint, row); }
   136	    row.count++;
   137	    row.bytesIn += bytesIn;
   138	    row.bytesOut += bytesOut;
   139	  }
   140	
   141	  setBaseUrl(url) {
   142	    this.baseUrl = (url || 'http://127.0.0.1:2223').replace(/\/$/, '');
   143	    this.healthCache = null;
   144	  }
   145	
   146	  _isLoopbackBaseUrl() {
   147	    return /^https?:\/\/(127\.0\.0\.1|localhost|\[::1\])(:\d+)?(\/|$)/i.test(this.baseUrl || '');
   148	  }
   149	
   150	  _isPrivatePath(path, payload = {}) {
   151	    if (typeof path === 'string' && path) {
   152	      // vault-relative (Clientes/...) OU absoluto/aninhado (/Users/.../Clientes/...)
   153	      if (/^Clientes\//i.test(path.replace(/^\/+/, ''))) return true;
   154	      if (/(^|\/)Clientes\//i.test(path)) return true;
   155	    }
   156	    if (payload && payload.privacy && /sigiloso/i.test(String(payload.privacy))) return true;
   157	    return false;
   158	  }
   159	
   160	  _assertRawContentAllowed(endpoint, options = {}) {
   161	    const privacyPath = options._privacyPath || options.privacyPath || options.path || null;
   162	    if (!this._isLoopbackBaseUrl() && this._isPrivatePath(privacyPath, options)) {
   163	      throw new Error(
   164	        `privacy-gate: ${endpoint} recusou enviar conteúdo sigiloso para daemon remoto (${this.baseUrl})`,
   165	      );
   166	    }
   167	  }
   168	
   169	  // Lazy health check — cached for HEALTH_TTL_MS
   170	  // v1.4.1 — timeoutMs (default 1500ms): probes precisam falhar rápido em URLs mortas
   171	  // para que discovery cross-device funcione sem travar Obsidian no startup.
   172	  async isAvailable(timeoutMs = 1500) {
   173	    const now = Date.now();
   174	    if (this.healthCache !== null && (now - this.healthCheckedAt) < this.HEALTH_TTL_MS) {
   175	      return this.healthCache;
   176	    }
   177	    try {
   178	      // Race a probe HTTP contra um timer — Obsidian's requestUrl não respeita AbortController,
   179	      // então usamos Promise.race como timeout externo.
   180	      const probe = this._requestUrl({
   181	        url: `${this.baseUrl}/v1/health`,
   182	        method: 'GET',
   183	        throw: false,
   184	      });
   185	      const timeout = new Promise(resolve =>
   186	        setTimeout(() => resolve({ status: 0, _timedOut: true }), timeoutMs)
   187	      );
   188	      const resp = await Promise.race([probe, timeout]);
   189	      const ok = resp && resp.status >= 200 && resp.status < 300;
   190	      this.healthCache = ok;
   191	    } catch {
   192	      this.healthCache = false;
   193	    }
   194	    this.healthCheckedAt = Date.now();
   195	    return this.healthCache;
   196	  }
   197	
   198	  // v2.0 — Inject PCC routing header into outgoing request headers.
   199	  _pccHeaders() {
   200	    if (this.pccMode === 'off') return {};
   201	    if (this.pccMode === 'auto') return { 'X-Zeus-Allow-Pcc': 'auto' };
   202	    return { 'X-Zeus-Allow-Pcc': '1' };  // opt-in
   203	  }
   204	
   205	  // v2.0 — Read PCC-routing signal from response headers.
   206	  // v1.15 — codex #5: o daemon sinaliza `X-Zeus-Pcc-Possible: 1` quando cloud era
   207	  // POSSÍVEL (heurística), não quando foi comprovadamente usado — Apple não expõe
   208	  // API de inspeção de routing.
   209	  _readPccPossible(headers) {
   210	    if (!headers) return false;
   211	    // Obsidian requestUrl returns headers as plain object; fetch returns Headers instance
   212	    const val = typeof headers.get === 'function'
   213	      ? headers.get('x-zeus-pcc-possible') || headers.get('X-Zeus-Pcc-Possible')
   214	      : (headers['x-zeus-pcc-possible'] || headers['X-Zeus-Pcc-Possible']);
   215	    const possible = val === '1' || val === 'true';
   216	    if (possible) this.pccPossibleCount++;
   217	    this.lastPccPossible = possible;
   218	    return possible;
   219	  }
   220	
   221	  // Try to load Obsidian's requestUrl from the obsidian module; fallback to fetch on Node
   222	  async _requestUrl({ url, method = 'GET', body, contentType = 'application/json', throw: throwOnError = true, signal = null }) {
   223	    let obsidian;
   224	    try { obsidian = require('obsidian'); } catch { obsidian = null; }
   225	
   226	    const pccHeaders = this._pccHeaders();
   227	
   228	    if (obsidian && obsidian.requestUrl) {
   229	      // Obsidian environment — preferred
   230	      const resp = await obsidian.requestUrl({
   231	        url, method, contentType,
   232	        headers: { 'Content-Type': contentType, ...pccHeaders },
   233	        body: typeof body === 'string' ? body : (body ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined),
   234	        throw: throwOnError,
   235	      });
   236	      this._readPccPossible(resp.headers);
   237	      return resp;
   238	    }
   239	
   240	    // Node fallback (testing, scripts)
   241	    if (typeof fetch === 'function') {
   242	      const resp = await fetch(url, {
   243	        method,
   244	        headers: { 'Content-Type': contentType, ...pccHeaders },
   245	        body: body ? (typeof body === 'string' ? body : JSON.stringify(body)) : undefined,
   246	        signal,
   247	      });
   248	      this._readPccPossible(resp.headers);
   249	      const text = await resp.text();
   250	      let json = null;
   251	      try { json = JSON.parse(text); } catch {}
   252	      return { status: resp.status, text, json, headers: resp.headers };
   253	    }
   254	
   255	    throw new Error('Nenhum transporte HTTP disponível (sem obsidian.requestUrl, sem fetch)');
   256	  }
   257

   260	    // não só /v1/embed. Deriva o path sensível do body (path/note_path/image_path)

    53	// === v0.12 PluginRequire helper ===
    54	// Obsidian plugin loader sets __dirname to Electron renderer init, not plugin dir.
    55	// Relative pluginRequire('lib/X') fails. Use absolute path via discovery.
    56	//
    57	// v1.4.2 — Discovery vault-agnóstica e device-agnóstica:
    58	//   1. __dirname / __filename quando o Electron loader os preserva
    59	//   2. Stack trace do próprio Error → extrai path do main.js em execução
    60	//   3. Glob de ~/Library/Mobile Documents/iCloud~md~obsidian/Documents/<qualquer-vault>/.obsidian/plugins/zeus
    61	//   4. Fallback final: paths conhecidos (Memoria + vault na raiz Documents)
    62	// Funciona em qualquer vault Obsidian/iCloud, em qualquer Mac, sem hardcoding.
    63	function _zeusFindPluginDir() {
    64	  // v1.4.1-ios — suporte a iOS: fs pode não existir no sandbox Capacitor
    65	  let fs0, path0;
    66	  try { fs0 = require('fs'); } catch (_) { fs0 = null; }
    67	  try { path0 = require('path'); } catch (_) { path0 = null; }
    68	
    69	  const isValid = (dir) => {
    70	    try {
    71	      if (!dir || !fs0) return false;
    72	      return fs0.existsSync(dir + '/main.js') && fs0.existsSync(dir + '/manifest.json');
    73	    } catch { return false; }
    74	  };
    75	
    76	  // 1) __dirname (macOS Electron preserva; iOS às vezes também)
    77	  try {
    78	    if (typeof __dirname === 'string' && isValid(__dirname)) return __dirname;
    79	  } catch (_) {}
    80	
    81	  // 2) Stack trace — regex com suporte a espaços no path (ex: "Mobile Documents")
    82	  // Corrige bug v1.4.0: [^():\s]+ cortava o path em "Mobile Documents" no iOS
    83	  try {
    84	    const stack = new Error().stack || '';
    85	    const re = /(?:\(|at\s+)((?:\/[^():\n]+)+\/main\.js):\d+(?::\d+)?\)?/g;
    86	    let m;
    87	    if (path0) {
    88	      while ((m = re.exec(stack)) !== null) {
    89	        const candidate = path0.dirname(m[1].trim());
    90	        if (isValid(candidate)) return candidate;
    91	      }
    92	    }
    93	  } catch (_) {}
    94	
    95	  // 3) iOS: sandbox path /private/var/mobile/Library/Mobile Documents/...
    96	  try {
    97	    if (fs0 && path0) {
    98	      const iosBases = [
    99	        '/private/var/mobile/Library/Mobile Documents/iCloud~md~obsidian/Documents',
   100	        '/var/mobile/Library/Mobile Documents/iCloud~md~obsidian/Documents',
   101	      ];
   102	      for (const base of iosBases) {
   103	        if (!fs0.existsSync(base)) continue;
   104	        const entries = fs0.readdirSync(base, { withFileTypes: true });
   105	        for (const e of entries) {
   106	          if (!e.isDirectory()) continue;
   107	          const candidate = `${base}/${e.name}/.obsidian/plugins/zeus`;
   108	          if (isValid(candidate)) return candidate;
   109	        }
   110	      }
   111	    }
   112	  } catch (_) {}
   113	
   114	  // 4) macOS: glob iCloud Drive do usuário
   115	  try {
   116	    if (fs0 && path0) {
   117	      const home = process.env.HOME || (process.env.USER ? '/Users/' + process.env.USER : '');
   118	      const iCloudBase = home + '/Library/Mobile Documents/iCloud~md~obsidian/Documents';
   119	      if (home && fs0.existsSync(iCloudBase)) {
   120	        const entries = fs0.readdirSync(iCloudBase, { withFileTypes: true });
   121	        for (const e of entries) {
   122	          if (!e.isDirectory()) continue;
   123	          const candidate = `${iCloudBase}/${e.name}/.obsidian/plugins/zeus`;
   124	          if (isValid(candidate)) return candidate;
   125	        }
   126	        const root = `${iCloudBase}/.obsidian/plugins/zeus`;
   127	        if (isValid(root)) return root;
   128	      }
   129	    }
   130	  } catch (_) {}
   131	
   132	  // 5) Fallbacks fixos macOS + iOS — derivados de $HOME (sem usernames hardcoded).
   133	  // v1.15 — codex #8: removidos paths pessoais /Users/<user>; reconstruímos a
   134	  // partir de process.env.HOME, que cobre qualquer usuário macOS. iOS usa o
   135	  // sandbox determinístico /private/var/mobile.
   136	  const home = (typeof process !== 'undefined' && process.env && process.env.HOME) || '';
   137	  const iCloudDocs = '/Library/Mobile Documents/iCloud~md~obsidian/Documents';
   138	  const fallback = [
   139	    '/private/var/mobile' + iCloudDocs + '/Memoria/.obsidian/plugins/zeus',
   140	    '/var/mobile' + iCloudDocs + '/Memoria/.obsidian/plugins/zeus',
   141	    home + iCloudDocs + '/Memoria/.obsidian/plugins/zeus',
   142	    home + iCloudDocs + '/.obsidian/plugins/zeus',
   143	  ];
   144	  for (const c of fallback) {
   145	    if (c && isValid(c)) return c;
   146	  }
   147	
   148	  // v1.4.3: sem fs (Capacitor) nao da pra VALIDAR caminhos — todas as 5
   149	  // estrategias acima usam fs0.existsSync, que nao existe no iOS. Retorna o
   150	  // caminho deterministico do sandbox iOS; o require() de pluginRequire confirma.
   151	  if (!fs0) {
   152	    return '/private/var/mobile/Library/Mobile Documents/iCloud~md~obsidian/Documents/Memoria/.obsidian/plugins/zeus';
   153	  }
   154	  throw new Error('Zeus pluginRequire: cannot locate plugin dir (procurei __dirname, stack, iOS sandbox, glob iCloud, fallbacks)');
   155	}
   156	const _ZEUS_PLUGIN_DIR = _zeusFindPluginDir();
   157	// v1.4.2-ios: require('path') unguarded crashava plugin no iPad/iPhone (Capacitor sandbox).
   158	let _zeusPath = null;
   159	try { _zeusPath = require('path'); } catch (_) { /* iOS sandbox — usa join string */ }
   160	function pluginRequire(rel) {
   161	  const full = (_zeusPath && _zeusPath.join)
   162	    ? _zeusPath.join(_ZEUS_PLUGIN_DIR, rel)
   163	    : (_ZEUS_PLUGIN_DIR + '/' + rel).replace(/\/+/g, '/');
   164	  return require(full);
   165	}

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba lib/daemon-lifecycle.js | sed -n '1,320p'" in /Users/rogermaiocchi/Code/zeus-obsidian-plugin/.claude/worktrees/gifted-poitras-209e91
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	/*
     2	 * daemon-lifecycle.js — auto-spawn do ZeusDaemonMac embarcado em bin/.
     3	 *
     4	 * Substitui o fluxo manual "rode install-mac-daemon.sh + launchctl" — o plugin
     5	 * Obsidian, ao carregar no Mac, sobe o daemon HTTP sozinho usando o binário
     6	 * em <plugin-dir>/bin/ZeusDaemonMac. iOS (Capacitor) pula porque não há
     7	 * child_process; cai automaticamente para o modo degradado read-only.
     8	 *
     9	 * Ordem de resolução do daemon:
    10	 *   1. /v1/health responde em http://127.0.0.1:2223 → reaproveita (LaunchAgent
    11	 *      pré-existente do dev, ou outra instância). Não spawna nada.
    12	 *   2. Spawna bin/ZeusDaemonMac em foreground (detached:false). O processo
    13	 *      filho é amarrado ao Obsidian — sair do Obsidian mata o daemon.
    14	 *   3. Polling em /v1/health por até 10s. Sucesso → registra como "spawnedByUs",
    15	 *      lifecycle:stop chama SIGTERM → SIGKILL.
    16	 *
    17	 * Tolerância: se faltar binário, child_process, ou se port 2223 estiver
    18	 * ocupado por outro processo, o módulo nunca lança — apenas retorna status
    19	 * negativo. O plugin continua funcionando com httpClient apontando para uma
    20	 * URL morta e degrada (resultados de busca semântica ficam vazios, mas o
    21	 * Obsidian não trava).
    22	 */
    23	
    24	'use strict';
    25	
    26	const BINARY_NAME = 'ZeusDaemonMac';
    27	const DEFAULT_PORT = 2223;
    28	const DEFAULT_HOST = '127.0.0.1';
    29	
    30	class DaemonLifecycle {
    31	  constructor(plugin, options = {}) {
    32	    this.plugin = plugin;
    33	    this.port = options.port || DEFAULT_PORT;
    34	    this.host = options.host || DEFAULT_HOST;
    35	    this.url = `http://${this.host}:${this.port}`;
    36	    this.child = null;
    37	    this.spawnedByUs = false;
    38	    this.lastStatus = null;
    39	    // v1.5.1 — fix codex MED: mutex para ensureRunning(). Sem isso, duas chamadas
    40	    // concorrentes (ex: onload race + status command paralelo) podem passar pelo
    41	    // health-check inicial e cada uma spawnar seu daemon — colisão na porta 2223.
    42	    this._startPromise = null;
    43	  }
    44	
    45	  _fs() { try { return require('fs'); } catch { return null; } }
    46	  _path() { try { return require('path'); } catch { return null; } }
    47	  _spawn() {
    48	    try { return require('child_process').spawn; } catch { return null; }
    49	  }
    50	  _execFileSync() {
    51	    try { return require('child_process').execFileSync; } catch { return null; }
    52	  }
    53	
    54	  binaryPath() {
    55	    const fs = this._fs();
    56	    const path = this._path();
    57	    if (!fs || !path) return null;
    58	    const vaultRoot = this.plugin.vaultRoot;
    59	    if (!vaultRoot || !this.plugin.manifest || !this.plugin.manifest.dir) return null;
    60	    const candidate = path.join(vaultRoot, this.plugin.manifest.dir, 'bin', BINARY_NAME);
    61	    return fs.existsSync(candidate) ? candidate : null;
    62	  }
    63	
    64	  async isHealthy(timeoutMs = 1500) {
    65	    const ZeusHttpClient = require('./zeus-http-client');
    66	    const probe = new ZeusHttpClient(this.url);
    67	    try { return await probe.isAvailable(timeoutMs); }
    68	    catch { return false; }
    69	  }
    70	
    71	  // Garante que o binário tem +x e sem quarantena (Gatekeeper).
    72	  // Idempotente — silencia falhas (codesign já é adhoc).
    73	  _prepareBinary(absPath) {
    74	    const fs = this._fs();
    75	    if (fs) {
    76	      try { fs.chmodSync(absPath, 0o755); } catch {}
    77	    }
    78	    const execFileSync = this._execFileSync();
    79	    if (execFileSync) {
    80	      try { execFileSync('/usr/bin/xattr', ['-d', 'com.apple.quarantine', absPath], { stdio: 'ignore' }); }
    81	      catch {}
    82	    }
    83	  }
    84	
    85	  async ensureRunning() {
    86	    // v1.5.1 — fix codex MED: serializa start. Promessa única reaproveitada
    87	    // por chamadas concorrentes até resolver (ou rejeitar).
    88	    if (this._startPromise) return this._startPromise;
    89	    this._startPromise = (async () => {
    90	      try { return await this._doEnsureRunning(); }
    91	      finally { this._startPromise = null; }
    92	    })();
    93	    return this._startPromise;
    94	  }
    95	
    96	  async _doEnsureRunning() {
    97	    if (await this.isHealthy(800)) {
    98	      this.lastStatus = { running: true, source: 'pre-existing', url: this.url };
    99	      return this.lastStatus;
   100	    }
   101	    const spawn = this._spawn();
   102	    if (!spawn) {
   103	      this.lastStatus = { running: false, source: 'no-spawn', reason: 'child_process unavailable (Capacitor / iOS)' };
   104	      return this.lastStatus;
   105	    }
   106	    const bin = this.binaryPath();
   107	    if (!bin) {
   108	      this.lastStatus = { running: false, source: 'no-binary', reason: `${BINARY_NAME} ausente em bin/` };
   109	      return this.lastStatus;
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    this._prepareBinary(bin);
   113	
   114	    return new Promise((resolve) => {
   115	      let resolved = false;
   116	      const finish = (status) => { if (!resolved) { resolved = true; this.lastStatus = status; resolve(status); } };
   117	
   118	      let child;
   119	      try {
   120	        child = spawn(bin, ['--port', String(this.port), '--host', this.host], {
   121	          stdio: 'ignore',
   122	          detached: false,
   123	          env: Object.assign({}, process.env || {}, { ZEUS_SPAWN_PARENT: 'obsidian' }),
   124	        });
   125	      } catch (e) {
   126	        finish({ running: false, source: 'spawn-error', reason: e.message });
   127	        return;
   128	      }
   129	
   130	      child.on('error', (err) => {
   131	        finish({ running: false, source: 'spawn-error', reason: err.message });
   132	      });
   133	      child.on('exit', (code, signal) => {
   134	        if (this.child === child) {
   135	          this.child = null;
   136	          this.spawnedByUs = false;
   137	        }
   138	        if (!resolved) finish({ running: false, source: 'spawn-exit', reason: `exit ${code} ${signal || ''}`.trim() });
   139	      });
   140	
   141	      this.child = child;
   142	      this.spawnedByUs = true;
   143	
   144	      const start = Date.now();
   145	      const poll = async () => {
   146	        if (resolved) return;
   147	        if (await this.isHealthy(600)) {
   148	          finish({ running: true, source: 'spawned', pid: child.pid, url: this.url, latencyMs: Date.now() - start });
   149	          return;
   150	        }
   151	        if (Date.now() - start > 10000) {
   152	          try { child.kill('SIGTERM'); } catch {}
   153	          finish({ running: false, source: 'spawn-timeout', reason: 'sem /v1/health em 10s' });
   154	          return;
   155	        }
   156	        setTimeout(poll, 300);
   157	      };
   158	      setTimeout(poll, 250);
   159	    });
   160	  }
   161	
   162	  async stop({ graceMs = 2000 } = {}) {
   163	    if (!this.spawnedByUs || !this.child) return { stopped: false, reason: 'not-spawned-by-us' };
   164	    const child = this.child;
   165	    this.child = null;
   166	    this.spawnedByUs = false;
   167	    // v1.5.1 — fix codex LOW: aguarda 'exit' do filho até graceMs. Só envia
   168	    // SIGKILL se SIGTERM não fechou o processo dentro da janela. Garante que
   169	    // shutdown gracioso do NIO/Swift complete antes de matar à força.
   170	    let exited = false;
   171	    const exitPromise = new Promise((resolve) => {
   172	      const onExit = () => { exited = true; resolve(); };
   173	      child.once('exit', onExit);
   174	      child.once('close', onExit);
   175	    });
   176	    try { child.kill('SIGTERM'); } catch {}
   177	    const timer = new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, graceMs));
   178	    await Promise.race([exitPromise, timer]);
   179	    if (!exited) {
   180	      try { child.kill('SIGKILL'); } catch {}
   181	      // pequena janela final para 'exit' depois do SIGKILL — útil para logs corretos.
   182	      await Promise.race([exitPromise, new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, 500))]);
   183	    }
   184	    return { stopped: true, force: !exited };
   185	  }
   186	}
   187	
   188	module.exports = DaemonLifecycle;

   322	// Sync sha256 using Node crypto when available; rolling-hash fallback on iOS
   323	// (iOS plugin only uses sha256 for content-change keys, not crypto-strong proofs).
   324	function sha256(text) {
   325	  if (universal.nodeCrypto && typeof universal.nodeCrypto.createHash === 'function') {
   326	    return universal.nodeCrypto.createHash('sha256').update(text).digest('hex');
   327	  }
   328	  let h = 0;
   329	  for (let i = 0; i < text.length; i++) h = ((h << 5) - h + text.charCodeAt(i)) | 0;
   330	  return (h >>> 0).toString(16).padStart(8, '0');
   331	}
   332	
   333	function cosine(a, b) {
   334	  let dot = 0, na = 0, nb = 0;
   335	  const len = Math.min(a.length, b.length);
   336	  for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) {
   337	    dot += a[i] * b[i]; na += a[i] * a[i]; nb += b[i] * b[i];
   338	  }
   339	  if (na === 0 || nb === 0) return 0;
   340	  return dot / (Math.sqrt(na) * Math.sqrt(nb));
   341	}
   342	
   343	function normalizeForMatch(s) {
   344	  return (s || '').toLowerCase().normalize('NFD').replace(/[̀-ͯ]/g, '');
   345	}

   347	function isMac() {
   348	  // process.platform doesn't exist on iOS (Capacitor) — fallback to UA detection.
   349	  return universal.isMacLike();
   350	}

   355	// Plugin v1.5 abandona o caminho child_process.spawn — toda operação Apple
   356	// passa pelo daemon HTTP local (bin/ZeusDaemonMac auto-spawned no Mac via
   357	// DaemonLifecycle, AegisDaemon embebido no host app no iOS). Retorna shape
   358	// { source, result } por compatibilidade com callsites legados.
   359	// -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   360	async function tryDaemonOrSpawn(plugin, daemonMethod, daemonArgs /* spawnArgs, stdinText, timeoutMs ignorados */) {
   361	  if (!plugin.httpClient || typeof plugin.httpClient[daemonMethod] !== 'function') {
   362	    throw new Error(`Daemon method indisponível: ${daemonMethod}`);
   363	  }
   364	  const reachable = await plugin.httpClient.isAvailable();
   365	  if (!reachable) {
   366	    throw new Error(`Daemon HTTP fora do ar (${plugin.httpClient.baseUrl}) — ${daemonMethod} não pôde rodar`);
   367	  }
   368	  const result = await plugin.httpClient[daemonMethod](...daemonArgs);
   369	  return { source: 'daemon', result };
   370	}
   371	
   372	// v1.15 — arquitetura ON-DEVICE pura (decisão do Roger: "autonomia própria, usar as
   373	// ferramentas do próprio OS"). Sem relay/mesh. Cada device usa o daemon Apple-nativo
   374	// LOCAL (loopback): macOS auto-spawna bin/ZeusDaemonMac; iOS, sem daemon on-device
   375	// (sandbox do plugin não roda código nativo), degrada para as lanes JS puras sobre os
   376	// índices computados no Mac e sincronizados via iCloud. NENHUMA topologia de rede no
   377	// fonte (removido o TAILSCALE_MESH hardcoded da auditoria v1.15) e nenhum peer remoto.
   378	
   379	// v1.4.1 — Per-device cache: localStorage não é sincronizado via iCloud, então cada device
   380	// memoriza sua própria URL funcional. Evita re-discovery em todo startup.
   381	//
   382	// IMPORTANTE — arquitetura on-device-first (Apple-native em TODOS os devices):
   383	//   macOS roda seu próprio daemon nativo em 127.0.0.1:2223 (ZeusDaemonMac, auto-spawn).
   384	//   iOS não roda daemon (sandbox) → degrada para JS puro sobre índices sincronizados.
   385	//   O cache só persiste loopback — não há rota remota.
   386	const ZEUS_LOCAL_DAEMON_KEY = 'zeus.daemon.url';        // cached URL string (sempre 127.0.0.1:* quando cacheado)
   387	const ZEUS_LOCAL_DAEMON_TS_KEY = 'zeus.daemon.ts';      // cached at (ms)
   388	const ZEUS_LOCAL_DAEMON_TTL_MS = 12 * 60 * 60 * 1000;   // 12h — re-probe periodicamente
   389	
   390	function _zeusIsLoopback(url) {
   391	  if (!url) return false;
   392	  return /^https?:\/\/(127\.0\.0\.1|localhost|\[::1\])(:\d+)?(\/|$)/i.test(url);
   393	}
   394	
   395	function _zeusGetLocalDaemonUrl() {
   396	  try {
   397	    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.localStorage) return null;
   398	    const url = window.localStorage.getItem(ZEUS_LOCAL_DAEMON_KEY);
   399	    const ts = parseInt(window.localStorage.getItem(ZEUS_LOCAL_DAEMON_TS_KEY) || '0', 10);
   400	    if (!url || !ts) return null;
   401	    if (Date.now() - ts > ZEUS_LOCAL_DAEMON_TTL_MS) return null;
   402	    return url;
   403	  } catch { return null; }
   404	}
   405	
   406	function _zeusSetLocalDaemonUrl(url) {
   407	  try {
   408	    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.localStorage) return;
   409	    if (!url) {
   410	      window.localStorage.removeItem(ZEUS_LOCAL_DAEMON_KEY);
   411	      window.localStorage.removeItem(ZEUS_LOCAL_DAEMON_TS_KEY);
   412	      return;
   413	    }
   414	    // Só cacheia loopback — URL remota não é "estado estável" do device.
   415	    if (!_zeusIsLoopback(url)) {
   416	      dbg('[zeus] cache skip — URL não é loopback (sempre re-probe local primeiro):', url);
   417	      return;
   418	    }
   419	    window.localStorage.setItem(ZEUS_LOCAL_DAEMON_KEY, url);
   420	    window.localStorage.setItem(ZEUS_LOCAL_DAEMON_TS_KEY, String(Date.now()));
   421	  } catch {}
   422	}
   423	
   424	// v1.4.1 — On-device-first daemon discovery.
   425	//
   426	// Ordem fixa de candidatos (ON-DEVICE puro — sem rota remota):
   427	//   1. 127.0.0.1:2223  — daemon LOCAL Apple-nativo (ZeusDaemonMac no Mac, auto-spawn)
   428	//   2. localhost:2223  — alternativa de hostname para o mesmo loopback
   429	//   3. settings.zeusDaemonUrl — override (default 127.0.0.1; sincronizado via iCloud)
   430	//
   431	// Probes em paralelo com timeout curto (1500ms); loopback sempre vence.
   432	async function discoverDaemonUrl(plugin, candidates = null, probeTimeoutMs = 1500) {
   433	  const ordered = [];
   434	  const seen = new Set();
   435	  const push = (u) => { if (u && !seen.has(u)) { seen.add(u); ordered.push(u); } };
   436	
   437	  if (candidates) {
   438	    for (const u of candidates) push(u);
   439	  } else {
   440	    // loopback primeiro (daemon local Apple-nativo daquele device), depois o override.
   441	    push('http://127.0.0.1:2223');
   442	    push('http://localhost:2223');
   443	    push(plugin.settings.zeusDaemonUrl);
   444	  }
   445	
   446	  const ZeusHttpClientLocal = require('./lib/zeus-http-client');
   447	  // Probe em paralelo — mas pondera resultado pela posição (loopback ganha de remoto).
   448	  const probes = ordered.map((url, idx) => (async () => {
   449	    try {
   450	      const client = new ZeusHttpClientLocal(url);
   451	      const ok = await client.isAvailable(probeTimeoutMs);
   452	      return ok ? { url, idx, loopback: _zeusIsLoopback(url) } : null;
   453	    } catch { return null; }
   454	  })());
   455	
   456	  const results = await Promise.allSettled(probes);
   457	  const winners = results
   458	    .filter(r => r.status === 'fulfilled' && r.value)
   459	    .map(r => r.value);
   460	
   461	  if (winners.length === 0) {
   462	    console.warn('[zeus] adaptive daemon discovery → NENHUM daemon respondeu (nem local nem mesh)');
   463	    return plugin.settings.zeusDaemonUrl;  // mantém o default para tentar de novo depois
   464	  }
   465	
   466	  // Prioriza loopback (on-device); se nenhum loopback, usa o de menor idx (mesh ordenado por proximidade).
   467	  const loopback = winners.find(w => w.loopback);
   468	  const chosen = loopback || winners.sort((a, b) => a.idx - b.idx)[0];
   469	
   470	  dbg('[zeus] adaptive daemon discovery → using', chosen.url,
   471	    chosen.loopback ? '(LOCAL on-device daemon ✓)' : '(REMOTE Tailscale fallback ⚠)');
   472	
   473	  _zeusSetLocalDaemonUrl(chosen.url);   // só cacheia se for loopback (helper filtra)
   474	  return chosen.url;
   475	}
   476	
   477	// Read Apple CoreSpotlight metadata via `mdls` — extract EXIF, GPS, dates, kind.
   478	// Mac-only — returns empty features on iOS (no child_process).
   479	async function acsMetadata(absPath) {
   480	  return new Promise((resolve) => {
   481	    if (!spawn) { resolve({}); return; }
   482	    const child = spawn('/usr/bin/mdls', ['-plist', '-', absPath], { stdio: ['ignore', 'pipe', 'pipe'] });
   483	    let out = '';
   484	    child.stdout.on('data', d => out += d.toString());
   485	    child.on('close', () => {
   486	      // Parse interesting attrs without full XML plist parsing
   487	      const features = {};
   488	      const wanted = [
   489	        'kMDItemKind', 'kMDItemContentTypeTree',
   490	        'kMDItemPixelWidth', 'kMDItemPixelHeight',
   491	        'kMDItemLatitude', 'kMDItemLongitude', 'kMDItemAltitude',
   492	        'kMDItemContentCreationDate', 'kMDItemContentModificationDate',
   493	        'kMDItemAcquisitionMake', 'kMDItemAcquisitionModel',
   494	        'kMDItemTitle', 'kMDItemAuthors', 'kMDItemNumberOfPages',
   495	        'kMDItemDescription', 'kMDItemUserTags', 'kMDItemFinderComment',
   496	      ];
   497	      for (const key of wanted) {
   498	        // Match <key>NAME</key>\s*<TYPE>VALUE</TYPE>
   499	        const re = new RegExp(`<key>${key}</key>\\s*<(string|real|integer|date)>([^<]+)</\\1>`);
   500	        const m = out.match(re);
   501	        if (m) features[key.replace('kMDItem', '')] = m[2];
   502	      }
   503	      resolve(features);
   504	    });
   505	    child.on('error', () => resolve({}));
   506	  });
   507	}

   526	  loadFromCache(sha) {
   527	    try {

   529	      if (!fs.existsSync(p)) return null;
   530	      return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(p, 'utf8'));
   531	    } catch { return null; }
   532	  }

     1	/*
     2	 * embed-ios.js — v1.12 embed-relay + iOS embed schema versionado.
     3	 *
     4	 * Codex audit v1.12 aprovou estratégia híbrida two-tier:
     5	 *
     6	 *   CAMADA 1 (default ON) — Relay Mac via Tailscale/loopback HTTP daemon
     7	 *     iOS chama daemon Mac (qualquer device com NLContextualEmbedding nativa) e

    12	 *   CAMADA 2 (opt-in labs, default OFF) — transformers.js + multilingual-e5-small

    23	 *   embeddings.jsonl  — 512-dim NLContextualEmbedding (Apple Mac/iOS daemon)

    33	 *       model_id: 'apple-nlcontextual-pt-BR' | 'Xenova/multilingual-e5-small',
    34	 *       model_revision: '...',         // commit/tag do modelo
    35	 *       dim: 512 | 384,                // recusa carregar se mismatch
    36	 *       device_class: 'mac' | 'ios' | 'ipad',
    37	 *       text_sha: '...',               // hash do texto embedado (não do file)
    38	 *       source: 'daemon-mac' | 'daemon-ios-relay' | 'transformers-ios',

    44	 * portanto seguro adicionar embeddings-ios como 7º retriever desde que cada
    45	 * device leia SÓ seu próprio jsonl (loader recusa dim mismatch).
    46	 */
    47	
    48	'use strict';
    49	
    50	const universal = require('./universal-fs');
    51	
    52	const EMBED_IOS_FILE = 'embeddings-ios.jsonl';
    53	const EMBED_IOS_DIM = 384;          // multilingual-e5-small
    54	const EMBED_IOS_MODEL = 'Xenova/multilingual-e5-small';
    55	const EMBED_MAC_DIM = 512;          // NLContextualEmbedding
    56	const EMBED_MAC_MODEL = 'apple-nlcontextual-pt-BR';
    57	
    58	class EmbedIos {
    59	  constructor(plugin) {
    60	    this.plugin = plugin;
    61	    this._entries = new Map();        // path → entry
    62	    this._loaded = false;
    63	    this._writePromise = null;        // mutex
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  get _adapter() { return this.plugin.app.vault.adapter; }
    67	  get dataPath() { return universal.joinPath(this.plugin.manifest.dir, 'data'); }
    68	  get jsonlPath() { return universal.joinPath(this.dataPath, EMBED_IOS_FILE); }
    69	
    70	  async load() {
    71	    if (this._loaded) return;
    72	    if (!(await universal.adapterExists(this._adapter, this.jsonlPath))) {
    73	      this._loaded = true;
    74	      return;
    75	    }
    76	    try {
    77	      const raw = await universal.adapterRead(this._adapter, this.jsonlPath);
    78	      for (const line of raw.split('\n').filter(Boolean)) {
    79	        try {
    80	          const obj = JSON.parse(line);
    81	          // codex MED: loader recusa dim mismatch (não truncar silente).
    82	          if (!obj || !obj.path) continue;
    83	          if (obj.dim !== EMBED_IOS_DIM) {
    84	            console.warn('[zeus.embed-ios] skip linha dim mismatch:', obj.path, 'dim=', obj.dim);
    85	            continue;
    86	          }
    87	          if (!Array.isArray(obj.vec) || obj.vec.length !== EMBED_IOS_DIM) {
    88	            console.warn('[zeus.embed-ios] skip linha vec inválida:', obj.path);
    89	            continue;
    90	          }
    91	          this._entries.set(obj.path, obj);
    92	        } catch (e) { /* skip malformed */ }
    93	      }
    94	    } catch (e) {
    95	      console.warn('[zeus.embed-ios] load failed:', e.message);
    96	    }
    97	    this._loaded = true;
    98	  }
    99	
   100	  // Get entry por path (iOS-local 384-dim).
   101	  async get(path) {
   102	    await this.load();
   103	    return this._entries.get(path) || null;
   104	  }
   105	
   106	  // Persist atomic. Mutex serializa concorrentes (v1.8.1 pattern).
   107	  async _persist() {
   108	    if (this._writePromise) await this._writePromise.catch(() => {});
   109	    this._writePromise = (async () => {
   110	      try {
   111	        await universal.adapterMkdir(this._adapter, this.dataPath);
   112	        const lines = [];
   113	        for (const e of this._entries.values()) lines.push(JSON.stringify(e));
   114	        await universal.adapterWriteAtomic(this._adapter, this.jsonlPath, lines.join('\n'));
   115	      } finally {
   116	        this._writePromise = null;
   117	      }
   118	    })();
   119	    return this._writePromise;
   120	  }
   121	
   122	  // Upsert entry. Validate schema + dim.
   123	  async upsert(entry) {
   124	    await this.load();
   125	    if (!entry || !entry.path) throw new Error('embed-ios.upsert: path obrigatório');
   126	    if (entry.dim !== EMBED_IOS_DIM) throw new Error(`embed-ios.upsert: dim ${entry.dim} ≠ ${EMBED_IOS_DIM}`);
   127	    if (!Array.isArray(entry.vec) || entry.vec.length !== EMBED_IOS_DIM) {
   128	      throw new Error('embed-ios.upsert: vec inválido');
   129	    }
   130	    // Garante schema fields obrigatórios
   131	    entry.schema = entry.schema || 'zeus-embeddings-v1';
   132	    entry.model_id = entry.model_id || EMBED_IOS_MODEL;
   133	    entry.created_at = entry.created_at || new Date().toISOString();
   134	    entry.source = entry.source || 'transformers-ios';
   135	    this._entries.set(entry.path, entry);
   136	    await this._persist();
   137	    return { upserted: entry.path, total: this._entries.size };
   138	  }
   139	
   140	  // Removes entry (note deleted/renamed)
   141	  async remove(path) {
   142	    await this.load();
   143	    if (this._entries.has(path)) {
   144	      this._entries.delete(path);
   145	      await this._persist();
   146	      return { removed: true };
   147	    }
   148	    return { removed: false };
   149	  }
   150	
   151	  // Stats
   152	  async stats() {
   153	    await this.load();
   154	    return {
   155	      schema: 'zeus-embeddings-v1',
   156	      file: this.jsonlPath,
   157	      model_id: EMBED_IOS_MODEL,
   158	      dim: EMBED_IOS_DIM,
   159	      count: this._entries.size,
   160	      runtime_installed: await this._modelInstalled(),
   161	    };
   162	  }
   163	
   164	  // Check se transformers.js + modelo estão instalados (cache local)
   165	  async _modelInstalled() {
   166	    // v1.12: detecção stub — checa se ~/.zeus-ios-embed-model/ existe no
   167	    // application support (futuro v1.13 labs gravará aqui após primeiro fetch).
   168	    // Por enquanto sempre retorna false (sem runtime instalado).
   169	    return false;
   170	  }
   171	
   172	  /**
   173	   * Embed um texto via transformers.js (lazy-load).
   174	   * v1.12 ENTREGA: stub que retorna instrução acionável quando runtime ausente.
   175	   * v1.13 labs implementará lazy-import xenova/transformers + modelo fetch.
   176	   */
   177	  async embedText(text) {
   178	    if (!(await this._modelInstalled())) {
   179	      throw new Error(
   180	        'embed-ios runtime não instalado. Rode comando "Zeus: instalar modelo iOS embed". '
   181	        + 'v1.12 ENTREGA é stub; runtime transformers.js completo em v1.13 labs (ADR-011).',
   182	      );
   183	    }
   184	    // TODO v1.13: const { pipeline } = await import('@xenova/transformers');
   185	    //             const ext = await pipeline('feature-extraction', EMBED_IOS_MODEL, { quantized: true });
   186	    //             const out = await ext('query: ' + text, { pooling: 'mean', normalize: true });
   187	    //             return Array.from(out.data);
   188	    throw new Error('embed-ios.embedText: runtime não implementado em v1.12');
   189	  }
   190	}
   191	
   192	// =========================================================================
   193	// EmbedRelay — camada 1 (preferida): tenta daemon HTTP via Tailscale/loopback.
   194	// Quando bem-sucedido, persiste no embeddings.jsonl Mac canônico (512-dim).
   195	// =========================================================================
   196	
   197	class EmbedRelay {
   198	  constructor(plugin) {
   199	    this.plugin = plugin;
   200	  }
   201	
   202	  /**
   203	   * Tenta embed via daemon HTTP (loopback Mac OU Tailscale relay iOS→Mac).
   204	   * Sucesso → retorna {ok: true, vec, dim, model, source}
   205	   * Falha → retorna {ok: false, reason}  (não lança — gracioso)
   206	   */
   207	  async tryEmbed(text, options = {}) {
   208	    if (!this.plugin.httpClient) return { ok: false, reason: 'no-httpClient' };
   209	    if (!text || text.length < 2) return { ok: false, reason: 'text-too-short' };
   210	    try {
   211	      const available = await this.plugin.httpClient.isAvailable(1500);
   212	      if (!available) return { ok: false, reason: 'daemon-unreachable' };
   213	      const r = await this.plugin.httpClient.embed(text, options);
   214	      const vec = (r && r.vectors && r.vectors[0]) || (r && r.vector) || null;
   215	      if (!Array.isArray(vec) || vec.length !== EMBED_MAC_DIM) {
   216	        return { ok: false, reason: `dim-mismatch: ${vec ? vec.length : 'null'}` };
   217	      }
   218	      return {
   219	        ok: true,
   220	        vec,
   221	        dim: EMBED_MAC_DIM,
   222	        model: (r && r.model) || EMBED_MAC_MODEL,
   223	        source: 'daemon-relay',
   224	      };
   225	    } catch (e) {
   226	      return { ok: false, reason: (e.message || String(e)).slice(0, 100) };
   227	    }
   228	  }
   229	}
   230	
   231	module.exports = EmbedIos;
   232	module.exports.EmbedRelay = EmbedRelay;
   233	module.exports.EMBED_IOS_DIM = EMBED_IOS_DIM;
   234	module.exports.EMBED_IOS_MODEL = EMBED_IOS_MODEL;
   235	module.exports.EMBED_MAC_DIM = EMBED_MAC_DIM;
   236	module.exports.EMBED_MAC_MODEL = EMBED_MAC_MODEL;

    67	   * Extract passport for a single note.
    68	   * Calls daemon /v1/passport/extract.
    69	   * Returns the passport object (also persisted to JSONL).
    70	   *
    71	   * v0.10: passport gains `sha` (sha256 of file content at extraction time),
    72	   * `extracted_by` (device_id from coordinator) and `extracted_at` (ISO timestamp)
    73	   * for cross-device staleness detection via PassportScheduler.
    74	   */
    75	  async buildOne(filePath, domainOptions = []) {
    76	    // v1.11 — Feature E: iOS-local fallback quando httpClient indisponível ou
    77	    // daemon fora do ar. Mantém o MESMO schema canônico de passports.jsonl
    78	    // (só model_versions.passport difere para auditoria).
    79	    //
    80	    // Decisão daemon vs local: prefere daemon (qualidade FM); cai para local
    81	    // se httpClient ausente OU isAvailable() falhar.
    82	    let daemonReachable = false;
    83	    if (this.plugin.httpClient && typeof this.plugin.httpClient.isAvailable === 'function') {
    84	      try {
    85	        daemonReachable = await this.plugin.httpClient.isAvailable(1500);
    86	      } catch { daemonReachable = false; }
    87	    }
    88	    if (!daemonReachable) {
    89	      return await this._buildOneLocal(filePath);
    90	    }
    91	    // Compute current SHA before daemon call so we can attach it to the passport
    92	    // even if the daemon doesn't return one.
    93	    let currentSha = null;
    94	    try {
    95	      // SHA precompute usa o vault-relative path; quando filePath é absoluto
    96	      // (Mac AutoIndexer), tenta extrair vault-relative removendo o vaultRoot.
    97	      const relForRead = this._vaultRelative(filePath);
    98	      if (relForRead && await universal.adapterExists(this._adapter, relForRead)) {
    99	        const content = await universal.adapterRead(this._adapter, relForRead);
   100	        currentSha = await universal.sha256Hex(content);
   101	      }
   102	    } catch (e) {
   103	      console.warn('[zeus][passport] sha precompute failed for', filePath, e.message);
   104	    }
   105	    let passport;
   106	    try {
   107	      passport = await this.plugin.httpClient.passportExtract(filePath, domainOptions);
   108	    } catch (e) {
   109	      // Daemon respondeu isAvailable mas /v1/passport/extract falhou — caímos
   110	      // para local mesmo assim, mantendo a promessa de "indexação never blocks".
   111	      console.warn('[zeus][passport] daemon extract failed, fallback to ios-local:', e.message);
   112	      return await this._buildOneLocal(filePath);
   113	    }
   114	    if (!passport || !passport.path) {
   115	      throw new Error(`PassportIndex.buildOne: resposta inválida para ${filePath}`);
   116	    }
   117	    // v1.15 — S8 Check 1: o daemon recebe absPath (Mac) e ecoa passport.path
   118	    // absoluto. Coage para vault-relative ANTES de virar chave do cache/JSONL,
   119	    // garantindo que o key do map case com o .path persistido (sem duplicatas).
   120	    passport.path = this._vaultRelative(passport.path);
   121	    // Stamp staleness-tracking fields (overwrite daemon-provided when we have local SHA).
   122	    if (currentSha) passport.sha = currentSha;
   123	    if (this.plugin.coordinator && this.plugin.coordinator.deviceId) {
   124	      passport.extracted_by = this.plugin.coordinator.deviceId;
   125	    }
   126	    passport.extracted_at = new Date().toISOString();
   127	    // Persist incrementally
   128	    const map = await this.loadAll();
   129	    map.set(passport.path, passport);
   130	    await this.saveAll(map);
   131	    // Mirror passport metadata into manifest for fast staleness scans.
   132	    try { await this._updateManifestEntry(passport); } catch (e) {
   133	      console.warn('[zeus][passport] manifest mirror failed:', e.message);
   134	    }
   135	    this._lastBuiltAt = new Date().toISOString();
   360	  // ---- Query (MCP-first surface) ----
   361	
   362	  /**
   363	   * Find passports semantically relevant to query.
   364	   * Delegates to daemon /v1/passport/find (which combines embeddings cosine + concept match).
   365	   *
   366	   * @param {string} query
   367	   * @param {object} options - { topN, minScore, conceptFilter, embeddingsPath, passportsPath }
   368	   * @returns {Promise<Array<passport>>}
   369	   */
   370	  async findByQuery(query, options = {}) {
   371	    // v1.11 Feature E — fallback iOS-local quando httpClient ausente OU daemon
   372	    // fora do ar. Reusa lib/bm25 + concept-overlap sobre passports.jsonl local.
   373	    let daemonReachable = false;
   374	    if (this.plugin.httpClient && typeof this.plugin.httpClient.isAvailable === 'function') {
   375	      try {
   376	        daemonReachable = await this.plugin.httpClient.isAvailable(1500);
   377	      } catch { daemonReachable = false; }
   378	    }
   379	    if (!daemonReachable) {
   380	      return await this.findByQueryLocal(query, options);
   381	    }
   382	    const dataDir = this.dataPath;
   383	    const opts = {
   384	      topN: options.topN || 10,
   385	      minScore: options.minScore || 0.3,
   386	      conceptFilter: options.conceptFilter || null,
   387	      embeddingsPath: options.embeddingsPath || universal.joinPath(dataDir, 'embeddings.jsonl'),
   388	      passportsPath: options.passportsPath || this.jsonlPath,
   389	    };
   390	    try {
   391	      const resp = await this.plugin.httpClient.passportFind(query, opts);
   392	      return (resp && resp.results) || (Array.isArray(resp) ? resp : []);
   393	    } catch (e) {
   394	      console.warn('[zeus][passport] daemon find failed, fallback to local:', e.message);
   395	      return await this.findByQueryLocal(query, options);
   396	    }
   397	  }

  1022	  // Lê conteúdo bruto do arquivo para o exact-match boost — só quando necessário.
  1023	  // Mac path: synchronous fs.readFileSync (fast, used in tight scoring loops).
  1024	  // iOS path: fs is null — caller has cache; readDoc returns '' (only impacts
  1025	  // the very rare "no qVec available" fallback, which can't happen on iOS since
  1026	  // daemon embed must succeed for search to work).
  1027	  readDoc(filePath) {
  1028	    try {
  1029	      if (!fs || !path) return '';
  1030	      const abs = path.join(this.plugin.vaultRoot, filePath);
  1031	      const content = fs.readFileSync(abs, 'utf8').replace(/^---\n[\s\S]*?\n---\n/, '');
  1032	      return content;
  1033	    } catch { return ''; }
  1034	  }
  1035	
  1036	  async embedQuery(query) {
  1037	    // v0.6 fase E++ — uniform HTTP-first via tryDaemonOrSpawn (works on Mac AND iOS)
  1038	    let textToEmbed = query;
  1039	    // HyDE: now also HTTP-first internally (HyDEExpander.expand uses tryDaemonOrSpawn)
  1040	    if (this.plugin.settings.hydeEnabled) {
  1041	      try {
  1042	        textToEmbed = await this.plugin.hyde.expand(query);
  1043	        dbg('[zeus] HyDE expansion (first 100):', textToEmbed.slice(0, 100));
  1044	      } catch (e) {
  1045	        console.warn('[zeus] HyDE failed, using raw query', e.message);
  1046	      }
  1047	    }
  1048	
  1049	    try {
  1050	      const r = await tryDaemonOrSpawn(
  1051	        this.plugin,
  1052	        'embed',
  1053	        [textToEmbed, { backend: this.plugin.settings.embedBackend }],
  1054	        ['embed', '--backend', this.plugin.settings.embedBackend],
  1055	        textToEmbed,
  1056	        25000
  1057	      );

  1059	        return (r.result && r.result.vectors && r.result.vectors[0]) || null;
  1060	      }
  1061	      const parsed = JSON.parse(r.result);
  1062	      return (parsed.vectors && parsed.vectors[0]) || null;
  1063	    } catch (e) {
  1064	      console.warn('[zeus] query embed failed (both paths)', e.message);
  1065	      return null;
  1066	    }
  1067	  }

  1069	  // Search principal: cosine semântico + exact-match boost
  1070	  async search(query, limit = 30) {
  1071	    if (!query || query.length < 2) return [];
  1072	    if (this.embeddings.size === 0) return [];
  1073	    const qNorm = normalizeForMatch(query);
  1074	
  1075	    // 1. Tentar embed da query — caminho semântico
  1076	    const qVec = await this.embedQuery(query);
  1077	
  1078	    // 2. Para cada doc, calcular score
  1079	    const results = [];
  1080	    for (const e of this.embeddings.values()) {
  1081	      if (!e.vec) continue;
  1082	      const semScore = qVec ? cosine(qVec, e.vec) : 0;
  1083	
  1084	      // exact-match boost: query (normalizada) aparece no título OU no body cache?

  1086	      // body só se sem qVec (fallback iOS).

  1089	      if (titleNorm.includes(qNorm)) exactHit = 1;

  1092	      if (!qVec && exactHit === 0) {
  1093	        const bodyNorm = normalizeForMatch(this.readDoc(e.path).slice(0, 30000));
  1094	        if (bodyNorm.includes(qNorm)) exactHit = 0.5;
  1095	      }

     1	// main.swift — ZeusDaemonMac
     2	//
     3	// Daemon macOS standalone que expõe inteligência on-device via HTTP loopback:
     4	//   POST /v1/embed     → NLContextualEmbedding (NaturalLanguage)
     5	//   POST /v1/ocr       → Vision VNRecognizeTextRequest
     6	//   POST /v1/summarize → FoundationModels LanguageModelSession (macOS 26+)
     7	//   POST /v1/enrich    → FoundationModels com contexto de vault
     8	//   GET  /v1/health    → status + plataforma + disponibilidade FM
     9	//   GET  /v1/tools     → lista de capacidades
    10	//
    11	// Contraparte Mac do AegisDaemon iOS (porta 2223), pensado para rodar como
    12	// LaunchAgent (~/Library/LaunchAgents/com.maiocchi.zeusdaemon.plist) no Mac mini.
    13	// Tríade Operacional: este é o tier 6 (on-device) da cascata Zeus quando o
    14	// conteúdo é confidencial/sigiloso e não pode sair do disco local.
    15	
    16	import Foundation
    17	import NIOCore
    18	import NIOPosix
    19	import NIOHTTP1
    20	#if canImport(Darwin)
    21	import Darwin
    22	#endif
    23	
    24	// MARK: - Argument parsing
    25	
    26	struct ZeusArgs {
    27	    // v1.14 — default loopback-only (codex CRIT #1). Bind seguro por padrão:
    28	    // o LaunchAgent/auto-spawn já passam --host 127.0.0.1. Para cross-device via
    29	    // Tailscale, exigir --host 0.0.0.0 EXPLÍCITO + ZEUS_DAEMON_TOKEN no ambiente
    30	    // (o handler recusa requisições não-loopback sem token — ver isAuthorized).
    31	    var host: String = "127.0.0.1"
    32	    var port: Int = 2223
    33	    var vaultPath: String? = nil
    34	
    35	    static func parse(_ argv: [String]) -> ZeusArgs {
    36	        var args = ZeusArgs()
    37	        var i = 1
    38	        while i < argv.count {
    39	            let a = argv[i]
    40	            switch a {
    41	            case "--port":
    42	                if i + 1 < argv.count, let p = Int(argv[i + 1]) { args.port = p; i += 1 }
    43	            case "--host":
    44	                if i + 1 < argv.count { args.host = argv[i + 1]; i += 1 }
    45	            case "--vault":
    46	                if i + 1 < argv.count { args.vaultPath = argv[i + 1]; i += 1 }
    47	            case "--help", "-h":
    48	                print("""
    49	                ZeusDaemonMac — Zeus on-device intelligence daemon (macOS)
    50	
    51	                Usage:
    52	                  ZeusDaemonMac [--port 2223] [--host 127.0.0.1] [--vault PATH]
    53	
    54	                Endpoints:
    55	                  GET  /v1/health
    56	                  GET  /v1/tools
    57	                  POST /v1/embed      {"text": "..."}
    58	                  POST /v1/ocr        {"image_path": "..."} or {"image_base64": "..."}
    59	                  POST /v1/summarize  {"text": "...", "max_tokens": 500}
    60	                  POST /v1/enrich     {"note_content": "...", "note_path": "..."}
    61	                """)
    62	                exit(0)
    63	            default:
    64	                FileHandle.standardError.write("[ZeusDaemonMac] aviso: argumento ignorado: \(a)\n".data(using: .utf8) ?? Data())
    65	            }
    66	            i += 1
    67	        }
    68	        return args
    69	    }
    70	}
    71	
    72	let args = ZeusArgs.parse(CommandLine.arguments)
    73	let vaultURL: URL? = args.vaultPath.map { URL(fileURLWithPath: $0) }
    74	
    75	// MARK: - Server bootstrap
    76	
    77	let group = MultiThreadedEventLoopGroup(numberOfThreads: 1)
    78	
    79	let bootstrap = ServerBootstrap(group: group)
    80	    .serverChannelOption(ChannelOptions.socketOption(.so_reuseaddr), value: 1)
    81	    .childChannelInitializer { channel in
    82	        channel.pipeline.configureHTTPServerPipeline(withErrorHandling: true).flatMap {
    83	            channel.pipeline.addHandler(ZeusMacHTTPHandler(vaultURL: vaultURL))
    84	        }
    85	    }
    86	    .childChannelOption(ChannelOptions.socketOption(.so_reuseaddr), value: 1)
    87	    .childChannelOption(ChannelOptions.maxMessagesPerRead, value: 1)
    88	
    89	let serverChannel: Channel
    90	do {
    91	    serverChannel = try bootstrap.bind(host: args.host, port: args.port).wait()
    92	} catch {
    93	    FileHandle.standardError.write("[ZeusDaemonMac] FATAL: bind \(args.host):\(args.port) falhou: \(error)\n".data(using: .utf8) ?? Data())
    94	    exit(2)
    95	}

   160	    typealias InboundIn = HTTPServerRequestPart
   161	    typealias OutboundOut = HTTPServerResponsePart
   162	
   163	    private var requestHead: HTTPRequestHead?
   164	    private var bodyBuffer: ByteBuffer?
   165	    private let vaultURL: URL?
   166	
   167	    init(vaultURL: URL?) {
   168	        self.vaultURL = vaultURL
   169	    }
   170	
   171	    // MARK: - Auth (v1.14 — codex CRIT #2/#3)
   172	    // Loopback é confiável (on-device-first). Requisições não-loopback exigem
   173	    // X-Zeus-Token igual a env ZEUS_DAEMON_TOKEN. Fail-closed: sem token
   174	    // configurado, todo peer remoto é recusado mesmo se bound em 0.0.0.0.
   175	    static func isLoopback(_ addr: SocketAddress?) -> Bool {
   176	        guard let ip = addr?.ipAddress else { return false }
   177	        return ip == "127.0.0.1" || ip == "::1" || ip == "::ffff:127.0.0.1"
   178	    }
   179	
   180	    static func isAuthorized(remote: SocketAddress?, head: HTTPRequestHead) -> Bool {
   181	        if isLoopback(remote) { return true }
   182	        guard let token = ProcessInfo.processInfo.environment["ZEUS_DAEMON_TOKEN"],
   183	              !token.isEmpty else { return false }
   184	        guard let provided = head.headers.first(name: "X-Zeus-Token")
   185	                ?? head.headers.first(name: "x-zeus-token") else { return false }
   186	        return constantTimeEquals(provided, token)
   187	    }
   188	
   189	    static func constantTimeEquals(_ a: String, _ b: String) -> Bool {
   190	        let ab = Array(a.utf8), bb = Array(b.utf8)
   191	        if ab.count != bb.count { return false }
   192	        var diff: UInt8 = 0
   193	        for i in 0..<ab.count { diff |= ab[i] ^ bb[i] }
   194	        return diff == 0
   195	    }
   196	
   197	    func channelRead(context: ChannelHandlerContext, data: NIOAny) {
   198	        switch self.unwrapInboundIn(data) {
   199	        case .head(let head):
   200	            self.requestHead = head
   201	            self.bodyBuffer = context.channel.allocator.buffer(capacity: 0)
   202	        case .body(var chunk):
   203	            if self.bodyBuffer == nil {
   204	                self.bodyBuffer = context.channel.allocator.buffer(capacity: chunk.readableBytes)
   205	            }
   206	            self.bodyBuffer?.writeBuffer(&chunk)
   207	        case .end:
   208	            self.handleRequest(context: context)
   209	        }
   210	    }
   211	
   212	    private func handleRequest(context: ChannelHandlerContext) {
   213	        guard let head = self.requestHead else {
   214	            self.writeJSON(context: context, status: .badRequest, dict: ["error": "missing request head"])
   215	            return
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        let bodyString: String
   219	        if var buf = self.bodyBuffer, buf.readableBytes > 0 {
   220	            bodyString = buf.readString(length: buf.readableBytes) ?? ""
   221	        } else {
   222	            bodyString = ""
   223	        }
   224	
   225	        self.requestHead = nil
   226	        self.bodyBuffer = nil
   227	
   228	        let path = head.uri.split(separator: "?").first.map(String.init) ?? head.uri
   229	        let method = head.method
   230	
   231	        if method == .OPTIONS {
   232	            var headers = HTTPHeaders()
   233	            headers.add(name: "Access-Control-Allow-Origin", value: "*")
   234	            headers.add(name: "Access-Control-Allow-Methods", value: "GET, POST, OPTIONS")
   235	            headers.add(name: "Access-Control-Allow-Headers", value: "Content-Type, X-Zeus-Allow-Pcc, X-Zeus-Token")
   236	            self.writeRaw(context: context, status: .noContent, headers: headers, body: nil)
   237	            return
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        // v1.14 — Auth gate (codex CRIT #2/#3). /v1/health aberto para discovery;
   241	        // todo o resto exige loopback OU X-Zeus-Token válido.
   242	        if path != "/v1/health" && !Self.isAuthorized(remote: context.remoteAddress, head: head) {
   243	            self.writeJSON(context: context, status: .unauthorized,
   244	                           dict: ["error": "unauthorized: non-loopback request requires valid X-Zeus-Token"])
   245	            return
   246	        }
   247	
   248	        // v1.15 — codex round 5 (debate iOS): defesa em profundidade para /v1/cmd.
   249	        // O endpoint de shell é LOOPBACK-ONLY: recusado para qualquer peer remoto
   250	        // MESMO com token válido. Blast radius alto demais para expor no relay
   251	        // Tailscale; o relay iOS→Mac precisa só dos endpoints Apple-native, não de
   252	        // exec de comandos. Mantém a superfície remota = inferência, não shell.
   253	        if path == "/v1/cmd" && !Self.isLoopback(context.remoteAddress) {
   254	            self.writeJSON(context: context, status: .forbidden,
   255	                           dict: ["error": "forbidden: /v1/cmd is loopback-only (não exposto a peers remotos, mesmo com token)"])
   256	            return
   257	        }
   258	
   259	        // v1.2 — PCC permission: extrair header X-Zeus-Allow-Pcc da request.
   260	        // Client envia "1" (opt-in per request) ou "auto" (sempre que daemon
   261	        // achar necessário). Default "off" preserva privacy gate on-device.
   262	        let pccHeaderValue = head.headers.first(name: "X-Zeus-Allow-Pcc")
   263	            ?? head.headers.first(name: "x-zeus-allow-pcc")
   264	        let pccPermission = PccPermission.fromHeader(pccHeaderValue)

codex
Há uma pendência mais séria que comentário: `lib/embed-ios.js` ainda mantém a classe `EmbedRelay` e o comando de status iOS ainda usa essa camada. Isso não parece conectado ao fluxo principal de discovery, mas é superfície de relay remanescente.
